[How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void\(0\))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ I wish I knew prior buying! ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/RKB1294KX7W6X/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on October 29, 2025
The media could not be loaded. 
We have purchased this fridge almost a year ago. Prior to this one we had the same fridge, but without the screen. It worked for us 13 years and still is, but we moved it to our second home and purchased new one for the primary residency.  
What we like:  
• The capacity is generous — ~29 cu ft of total storage gives plenty of room for a family of 10, which is great when you have kids, snacks, and healthy foods.  
• Excellent flexibility: the “FlexZone” lower‑right compartment lets you switch between refrigerator or freezer mode; the Beverage Center + internal water dispenser + auto‑fill pitcher are super convenient for water, kids’ drinks, etc.  
• Smart features: we weren’t interested in those too much, but we live calendar, weather, drawing pad for the toddler-suddenly got very popular  
• they say it’s finger print resistant- Not sure where they getting it- it has millions of fingerprints on ours 😂 may be fridge resists to some, not here  
  
Things to consider:  
• Size & clearance: The fridge is deep (~34¼″ plus door swing) and tall (~73″), so you’ll want to measure your space- IT IS bigger then your normal fridge  
• Cost & value: This is a premium fridge with premium price. But you will use it every single day for many years.. it’s way worth buying a quality item  
• Service & complexity: we never had issues, ever  
Summary verdict:  
  
If you’re looking for a top‑of‑the‑line refrigerator for your home and will use many of its smart features and flexible zones, then this Samsung model is an excellent choice: it looks great, works well, and gives you a lot of modern functionality. On the other hand, if your space is tighter, or your budget is more modest, or you prefer simplicity and ultra‑reliability over features, you might consider a less expensive model with fewer bells and whistles.
